class="ajax__tab_panel" style="visibility: visible;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures_ProductFeatureDesc"><span class="h1"><strong style="color: #000000;">Ruger</strong></span> <h2><font style="color: #000000;"><strong><span>BX-25 Magazine For Model 10/22, 77/22, SR-22 and 22 Charger .22 Long Rifle 25 Rounds</span></strong></font></h2> <p><strong><span>&nbsp;</span><font face="book antiqua,palatino" size="3">This genuine Ruger factory magazine with Ruger logo has been tested and has proven to feed as reliably as the standard 10-round Ruger rotary magazine. BX-25 magazines will work with any factory original Ruger 10/22 rifle, SR-22 rifle, and 22 Charger pistol.</font></strong></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><font size="2"><span style="font-size: 8pt;">Designed by Ruger engineers for perfect and reliable function in any of the many 10/22 rifle models. Factory manufacturing and Ruger quality controls guarantee excellent fit and operation.&nbsp;</span></font></p> <p><br><font size="2">This magazine includes a polymer body and magazine follower. The steel feeding lips are designed for thousands of rounds- without any noticeable wear- meaning a you can shoot all you want. Keep a few spare mags in your kit; extra magazines save precious time at the range. Never be without a <strong>"ready to shoot"</strong> hi cap magazine at hand!</font></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <table class="root" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" align="center"> <tbody> <tr> <td class="content"> <p class="newsBig"><font style="color: #ff0000;"><span class="headline">Ruger Introduces 25-Round Magazine for Ruger 10/22</span>&nbsp;</font><br><font style="color: #ff0000;"><span class="date">April 29, 2011</span>&nbsp;</font><br><font style="color: #ff0000;"><span class="Copy">Sturm, Ruger &amp; Company, Inc. (NYSE: RGR) announces that owners of America's most popular autoloading rimfire rifle, the Ruger® 10/22®, can enjoy the extended fun offered by the new 25-round BX-25™ magazine. The new, genuine Ruger BX-25 magazine features the same correct angle feed lips that deliver the famous reliability of factory BX-1™ 10-round rotary magazines.<br><br>The BX-25 magazine will work in all vintages of Ruger 10/22 and SR-22® rifles, as well as all Ruger Charger™ pistols. The BX-25 magazines have stainless steel feed lips and use a stainless steel "constant force" spring. The anti-tilt follower is injection molded from Celcan - a high lubricity polyacetal. The magazine body halves are injection molded from durable glass-filled nylon.<br><br>"These are genuine Ruger factory magazines. We designed them. We didn't license and rebrand someone else's magazines," said Ruger CEO Michael Fifer. "We tested the BX-25 magazines extensively and they work as well as the original Ruger BX-1 rotary magazine, the gold standard for rimfire autoloading reliability," he continued.<br><br>The Ruger 10/22 is available in many configurations, including the special edition officially licensed Ruger Boy Scout™ 10/22 Rifle. Millions of shooters worldwide have learned the basics of firearms safety and marksmanship using a Ruger 10/22. It is a favorite of small bore hunters, competitive shooters and target shooters everywhere. Over six million Ruger 10/22's have been produced since it was introduced in 1964.</span></font></p> </td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>&nbsp;</p></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications_ProductsSpecifications"><ul><li>Category : Magazines and Accessories</li><li>Caliber : 22 Long Rifle</li><li>Capacity : 25 rd</li><li>Finish : Black</li><li>Model : 10/22 BX-25</li><li>Material : Polymer</li><li>Type : Detachable</li><li>Model Fit : 10/22 Series</li><li>Brand Fit : Ruger</li></ul></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Reviews"> <div id="Review"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_UpdatePnlProductReviewDetails"> <div class="Sorting"> <span class="TitleStyle"> Reviewed by <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_CustomersCnt">5</span> customer </span>&nbsp;
